// ==================== src\utils\messageFormatter.ts ====================
interface FormattedSegment {
    type: 'text' | 'bold' | 'italic' | 'underline' | 'link' | 'image' | 'video';
    content: string;
    url?: string;
    alt?: string;
}

export class MessageFormatter {
    private static readonly PATTERNS = {
        BOLD: /\*\*(.*?)\*\*/g,
        ITALIC: /\*(.*?)\*/g,
        UNDERLINE: /__(.*?)__/g,
        LINK: /\[(.*?)\]\((https?:\/\/[^\s<>[\]()]+)\)/g,
        IMAGE: /!image\[\](https?:\/\/[^\s<>[\]()]+)/g,
        VIDEO: /!video\[\](https?:\/\/(?:www\.)?youtube\.com\/watch\?v=([a-zA-Z0-9_-]+))/g
    };

    private static readonly URL_REGEX = /^https?:\/\/[^\s<>[\]()]+$/;
    private static readonly ALLOWED_IMAGE_EXTENSIONS = ['.jpg', '.jpeg', '.png', '.gif', '.webp', '.mp4'];
    private static readonly MAX_IMAGE_SIZE = 5 * 1024 * 1024; // 5MB

    /**
     * Parses a message into segments that can be rendered
     */
    public static parseMessage(message: string): FormattedSegment[] {
        const segments: FormattedSegment[] = [];
        let remainingText = message;
        let lastIndex = 0;

        // Helper function to add plain text segment
        const addTextSegment = (text: string) => {
            if (text) {
                segments.push({ type: 'text', content: text });
            }
        };

        // Process each pattern
        while (lastIndex < remainingText.length) {
            let earliestMatch: { pattern: RegExp; type: string; index: number; match: RegExpExecArray } | null = null;

            // Find the earliest match among all patterns
            for (const [key, pattern] of Object.entries(MessageFormatter.PATTERNS)) {
                pattern.lastIndex = lastIndex;
                const match = pattern.exec(remainingText);
                if (match && (!earliestMatch || match.index < earliestMatch.index)) {
                    earliestMatch = {
                        pattern,
                        type: key.toLowerCase(),
                        index: match.index,
                        match
                    };
                }
            }

            if (!earliestMatch) {
                // No more patterns found, add remaining text
                addTextSegment(remainingText.slice(lastIndex));
                break;
            }

            // Add text before the match
            addTextSegment(remainingText.slice(lastIndex, earliestMatch.index));

            // Process the match based on its type
            switch (earliestMatch.type) {
                case 'bold':
                    segments.push({
                        type: 'bold',
                        content: earliestMatch.match[1]
                    });
                    break;
                case 'italic':
                    segments.push({
                        type: 'italic',
                        content: earliestMatch.match[1]
                    });
                    break;
                case 'underline':
                    segments.push({
                        type: 'underline',
                        content: earliestMatch.match[1]
                    });
                    break;
                case 'link':
                    if (this.isValidUrl(earliestMatch.match[2])) {
                        segments.push({
                            type: 'link',
                            content: earliestMatch.match[1],
                            url: earliestMatch.match[2]
                        });
                    } else {
                        addTextSegment(earliestMatch.match[0]);
                    }
                    break;
                case 'image':
                    if (this.isValidImageUrl(earliestMatch.match[1])) {
                        segments.push({
                            type: 'image',
                            content: '',
                            url: earliestMatch.match[1]
                        });
                    } else {
                        addTextSegment(earliestMatch.match[0]);
                    }
                    break;
                case 'video':
                    if (this.isValidYoutubeUrl(earliestMatch.match[1])) {
                        segments.push({
                            type: 'video',
                            content: '',
                            url: `https://www.youtube.com/embed/${earliestMatch.match[2]}`
                        });
                    } else {
                        addTextSegment(earliestMatch.match[0]);
                    }
                    break;
            }

            lastIndex = earliestMatch.index + earliestMatch.match[0].length;
        }

        return segments;
    }

    /**
     * Validates a URL string
     */
    private static isValidUrl(url: string): boolean {
        try {
            new URL(url);
            return MessageFormatter.URL_REGEX.test(url);
        } catch {
            return false;
        }
    }

    /**
     * Validates an image URL
     */
    private static isValidImageUrl(url: string): boolean {
        if (!this.isValidUrl(url)) return false;
        return MessageFormatter.ALLOWED_IMAGE_EXTENSIONS.some(ext => 
            url.toLowerCase().endsWith(ext)
        );
    }

    /**
     * Validates a YouTube URL
     */
    private static isValidYoutubeUrl(url: string): boolean {
        return this.isValidUrl(url) && url.includes('youtube.com/watch?v=');
    }

    /**
     * Sanitizes text content to prevent XSS
     */
    public static sanitizeText(text: string): string {
        return text
            .replace(/&/g, '&amp;')
            .replace(/</g, '&lt;')
            .replace(/>/g, '&gt;')
            .replace(/"/g, '&quot;')
            .replace(/'/g, '&#039;');
    }

    /**
     * Formats a message for display, returning an array of segments
     */
    public static formatMessage(message: string): FormattedSegment[] {
        // First sanitize the raw text
        const sanitizedMessage = this.sanitizeText(message);
        // Then parse the formatting
        return this.parseMessage(sanitizedMessage);
    }
}

export type { FormattedSegment };


// ==================== src\workers\chat.worker.ts ====================
import * as signalR from '@microsoft/signalr';
import type { 
    TabInfo, 
    BroadcastMessage, 
    ChatMessage, 
    RetryContext, 
    ConnectionStatus 
} from '../types/chat';

class ChatConnectionManager {
    private connection: signalR.HubConnection | null = null;
    private activeTabs: Map<string, TabInfo> = new Map();
    private broadcastChannel: BroadcastChannel;
    private reconnectAttempts: number = 0;
    private readonly MAX_RECONNECT_ATTEMPTS = 5;
    private readonly PING_INTERVAL = 30000; // 30 seconds
    private readonly TAB_TIMEOUT = 45000; // 45 seconds

    constructor() {
        this.broadcastChannel = new BroadcastChannel('shinobi-rift-chat');
        this.setupBroadcastListener();
        this.startPingInterval();
    }

    private setupBroadcastListener(): void {
        this.broadcastChannel.onmessage = (event: MessageEvent<BroadcastMessage>) => {
            switch (event.data.type) {
                case 'ping':
                    this.handleTabPing(event.data.data);
                    break;
                case 'message':
                    this.broadcastToOtherTabs(event.data);
                    break;
            }
        };
    }

    private startPingInterval(): void {
        setInterval(() => {
            this.cleanupInactiveTabs();
        }, this.PING_INTERVAL);
    }

    private cleanupInactiveTabs(): void {
        const now = Date.now();
        for (const [tabId, info] of this.activeTabs.entries()) {
            if (now - info.lastPing > this.TAB_TIMEOUT) {
                this.activeTabs.delete(tabId);
                if (info.isActive) {
                    // If we lost the active tab, promote another tab
                    this.promoteNewActiveTab();
                }
            }
        }
    }

    private promoteNewActiveTab(): void {
        if (this.activeTabs.size === 0) return;

        // Find the tab with the most recent ping
        let mostRecentTab: [string, TabInfo] | null = null;
        for (const entry of this.activeTabs.entries()) {
            if (!mostRecentTab || entry[1].lastPing > mostRecentTab[1].lastPing) {
                mostRecentTab = entry;
            }
        }

        if (mostRecentTab) {
            const [tabId, info] = mostRecentTab;
            info.isActive = true;
            this.activeTabs.set(tabId, info);
            this.broadcastChannel.postMessage({
                type: 'status',
                data: { tabId, isActive: true }
            } as BroadcastMessage);
        }
    }

    private handleTabPing(data: { tabId: string; isActive: boolean }): void {
        const { tabId, isActive } = data;
        const existingTab = this.activeTabs.get(tabId);
        const now = Date.now();

        if (existingTab) {
            // Update existing tab
            existingTab.lastPing = now;
            if (existingTab.isActive !== isActive) {
                existingTab.isActive = isActive;
                if (isActive) {
                    // Deactivate all other tabs
                    for (const [otherTabId, info] of this.activeTabs.entries()) {
                        if (otherTabId !== tabId && info.isActive) {
                            info.isActive = false;
                            this.activeTabs.set(otherTabId, info);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            this.activeTabs.set(tabId, existingTab);
        } else {
            // Register new tab
            this.activeTabs.set(tabId, {
                id: tabId,
                isActive,
                lastPing: now
            });

            // If this is the first tab, make it active
            if (this.activeTabs.size === 1) {
                const tab = this.activeTabs.get(tabId)!;
                tab.isActive = true;
                this.activeTabs.set(tabId, tab);
            }
        }

        // Ensure connection is established if we have any tabs
        if (this.activeTabs.size > 0 && !this.connection) {
            this.initializeConnection();
        }
    }

    private async initializeConnection(): Promise<void> {
        try {
            this.connection = new signalR.HubConnectionBuilder()
                .withUrl('/chat')
                .withAutomaticReconnect({
                    nextRetryDelayInMilliseconds: (retryContext: RetryContext) => {
                        if (retryContext.previousRetryCount >= this.MAX_RECONNECT_ATTEMPTS) {
                            return null; // Stop retrying
                        }

                        // Exponential backoff
                        return Math.min(1000 * Math.pow(2, retryContext.previousRetryCount), 30000);
                    }
                })
                .build();

            this.setupConnectionHandlers();
            await this.connection.start();
            this.reconnectAttempts = 0;

            this.broadcastChannel.postMessage({
                type: 'status',
                data: { connected: true } as ConnectionStatus
            } as BroadcastMessage);
        } catch (error) {
            const errorMessage = error instanceof Error ? error : new Error('Failed to initialize connection');
            this.handleConnectionError(errorMessage);
        }
    }

    private setupConnectionHandlers(): void {
        if (!this.connection) return;

        this.connection.on('ReceiveMessage', (message: ChatMessage) => {
            this.broadcastChannel.postMessage({
                type: 'message',
                data: message
            } as BroadcastMessage);
        });

        this.connection.onclose((error?: Error) => {
            if (error) {
                this.handleConnectionError(error);
            }
        });
    }

    private handleConnectionError(error: Error): void {
        this.reconnectAttempts++;
        this.broadcastChannel.postMessage({
            type: 'error',
            data: {
                message: error.message || 'Connection error',
                error: {
                    name: error.name,
                    message: error.message,
                    stack: error.stack
                },
                attemptingReconnect: this.reconnectAttempts < this.MAX_RECONNECT_ATTEMPTS
            }
        } as BroadcastMessage);

        if (this.reconnectAttempts < this.MAX_RECONNECT_ATTEMPTS) {
            setTimeout(() => {
                this.initializeConnection();
            }, Math.min(1000 * Math.pow(2, this.reconnectAttempts), 30000));
        }
    }

    private broadcastToOtherTabs(message: BroadcastMessage): void {
        // Only broadcast messages from the active tab
        const hasActiveTab = Array.from(this.activeTabs.values()).some(tab => tab.isActive);
        if (!hasActiveTab) {
            this.promoteNewActiveTab();
        }
    }

    public async sendMessage(message: ChatMessage): Promise<void> {
        if (!this.connection) {
            throw new Error('No connection available');
        }

        try {
            await this.connection.invoke('SendMessage', message);
        } catch (error) {
            const errorMessage = error instanceof Error ? error : new Error('Failed to send message');
            this.handleConnectionError(errorMessage);
            throw errorMessage;
        }
    }
}

// Initialize the connection manager
const chatManager = new ChatConnectionManager();

// Handle messages from tabs
self.onmessage = async (event: MessageEvent) => {
    const { type, data } = event.data;

    switch (type) {
        case 'send':
            try {
                await chatManager.sendMessage(data);
            } catch (error) {
                self.postMessage({
                    type: 'error',
                    data: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error occurred'
                });
            }
            break;
    }
};

// Ensure TypeScript recognizes this as a module
export {};
